              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12699084383288568387"><b>
  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br/><br/>I was very much looking forward to reading the books from Remy's POV, that was, until the reviews/ratings started coming in. It really seems to boil down to whether you love it or...don't love it. <br/><br/>If you've read any of the books, you know that Remy is intense and he is very primal. If the licking and scenting turned you off, you really won't like it hearing it from him. I was surprised that it didn't bother me considering I thought the licking and scenting was a bit much. But for</span>
  <span id="freeText12699084383288568387" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>My Thoughts:</u>
</b><br><br>I was very much looking forward to reading the books from Remy's POV, that was, until the reviews/ratings started coming in. It really seems to boil down to whether you love it or...don't love it. <br><br>If you've read any of the books, you know that Remy is intense and he is very primal. If the licking and scenting turned you off, you really won't like it hearing it from him. I was surprised that it didn't bother me considering I thought the licking and scenting was a bit much. But for some reason, I just <i>got it</i> reading it from his POV. His intensity just made more sense coming from him - the way he thought and the way he felt. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1385363241ra/7133494.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Of course, sometimes he seems very simple minded...thinking of Brooke or fighting or thinking of Brooke while he is fighting. And naturally when he's thinking of Brooke, he's thinking of having sex with her, <i>excuse me</i>, "mating" with her...or licking and scenting her. ;) Then seemingly out of left field, he will answer something with amazing clarity and foresight. <br><br>But I did like reading about his feelings and how he tried to come to terms with his feelings for Brooke and her feelings for him...something more than sex, something he's never had before. I love how he always turns to music and how music has always been there for him. I also loved how just seeing Brooke helped calm him. <br><br>I was hoping to get more insight on his feelings after the first big fight and the drama but unfortunately, he was black.<br><br>Most of the story is told in Remy's POV of scenes from the past but we do get several chapters of the present and I really enjoyed those. I can't really say spoilers but I like seeing how he is in a certain role. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379786887i/488833.jpg" width="350" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><br>Whether you love it...or don't love it, one thing is for sure, there is no other series out there like this - at least that I've read. Remy is definitely unique. <br><br>I just noticed that the next two books have been switched around...I guess Melanie's boyfriend is a handful and KE is having to rewrite so Melanie's book, <i>Raw</i>, will be last. The next book will be <i>Ripped</i> with a friend of Brooke's called Pandora. Hopefully we will get a bit of Brooke and Remy in that one!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385709433i/7207272._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="050" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>ღ “It means I’m going French this week and not showering so I can smell you on me.” <br><br>God, I swear only my woman would say that."<br><br>ღ “Protecting you is my <i>privilege</i>. I will protect you and anything that <i>you</i> value as if it were <i>mine</i>.”<br><br>ღ "Whatever it's on, it means it's yours."</span>
  <a data-text-id="12699084383288568387" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_595200849" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/595200849" />
    <a title="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9816167-jessica-s-book-review"><img alt="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1454474452p2/9816167.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/595200849?book_show_action=true">Apr 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica&#39;s Book Review" href="/user/show/9816167-jessica-s-book-review">Jessica&#39;s Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer595200849" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3195927170315138845">Remy has always been mysterious to me… he is a man of a few words, he grunts a lot, shares his feelings through music and now in Remy we get to know what he is thinking, what he is really feeling, what he is really scared of. Remy is a much more darker character then we ever knew.<br/><br/>Remy is a perfect mix of flash backs as well as present scenes. I think my absolute favorite thing was getting into Remy’s head the first time he saw Brooke at the match in Real. I think we can all agree when Remy took </span>
  <span id="freeText3195927170315138845" style="display:none">Remy has always been mysterious to me… he is a man of a few words, he grunts a lot, shares his feelings through music and now in Remy we get to know what he is thinking, what he is really feeling, what he is really scared of. Remy is a much more darker character then we ever knew.<br><br>Remy is a perfect mix of flash backs as well as present scenes. I think my absolute favorite thing was getting into Remy’s head the first time he saw Brooke at the match in Real. I think we can all agree when Remy took off in the middle of the ring to chase after Brooke was one of the sexiest, hottest, alpha male scenes EVER in the history of books. I loved being to know what Remy was thinking and feeling. It’s like he almost knew he loved Brooke just by see her even if he did not know what love was at the time.<br><br>I always liked Remy but being able to know his thoughts and feelings only made me love him more. He maybe has some issues but deep down he just wanted what was his and that was Brooke. Remy felt like a big bonus to me and I am so glad I was able to read it. I am also glad that the book wasn’t too long. It was the perfect length… sometimes I felt in the first two books things were written in just to make it longer but Remy was perfect.<br><br>I give Remy (Real #3) 4 Stars.<br><br><i>Book provided by the author in return for an honest review.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382766162i/6182035.png" width="190" height="119" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Stay connected with my reviews, book news and more:<br><a href="http://jessicasbookreview.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog- Jessica’s Book Review</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/JessicasBookReview" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/jessbookreview" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> </b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3195927170315138845" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_751134662" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/751134662" />
    <a title="Suzy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10559771-suzy"><img alt="Suzy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565972341p2/10559771.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/751134662?book_show_action=true">Oct 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suzy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suzy" href="/user/show/10559771-suzy">Suzy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10559771-suzy?shelf=drivel">drivel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10559771-suzy?shelf=slap-that-heroine">slap-that-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10559771-suzy?shelf=whole-lotta-meh">whole-lotta-meh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10559771-suzy?shelf=did-not-finish">did-not-finish</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10559771-suzy?shelf=switch-pov-nightmare">switch-pov-nightmare</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10559771-suzy?shelf=why-why-why">why-why-why</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer751134662" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14840091875708273245">DNF @ 27%% - actually <b>COULD</b> not finish <br/><br/>Okay so because I shelved Remy as a DNF I can't actually review it but I CAN give my observations and my general feelings so here go....<br/><br/>I <b>tried</b> and <b>tried</b> to push my way through Remy, I really did but I cannot & will not force myself to read anymore. In my opinion, this book is bad, <i>very, very bad</i>. I desperately wanted it to be good because Real was actually one of my favorite books of 2013. What I got was a poorly written, ham fisted, abomination of a book.</span>
  <span id="freeText14840091875708273245" style="display:none">DNF @ 27%% - actually <b>COULD</b> not finish <br /><br />Okay so because I shelved Remy as a DNF I can't actually review it but I CAN give my observations and my general feelings so here go....<br /><br />I <b>tried</b> and <b>tried</b> to push my way through Remy, I really did but I cannot &amp; will not force myself to read anymore. In my opinion, this book is bad, <i>very, very bad</i>. I desperately wanted it to be good because Real was actually one of my favorite books of 2013. What I got was a poorly written, ham fisted, abomination of a book. Being that this book was REAL &amp; MINE from Remys POV, I knew that the story was going to rehash a lot that I'd already read but I was excited to get into Remingtons head - unfortunately Remy sounded exactly the same as Brooke with the exception that Remington say "fuck" more - 557 times apparently. There is absolutely no insight into why Remy does what he does, says what he says or feels the way he feels. The repetition of words, <b>scenting - mine - speedy - licking</b>, and phrases was excruciating. I'm sorry, but I think in this instance Ms Evans should have stopped while she was ahead instead of spreading her original idea so thinly that her characters became unlikable douchecanoes.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14840091875708273245" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CnOW3aA8LJ7ilviIcQhZJ42DXiOLVkfqVrj90KFz04cwVf8PG2Ll9kW9TOmG/VP4W9y560XbyY0NxrthbDAhHQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('qQrJL5OIk5jE8RxRh8XXoXj7EjdGzrCNItN3zZcO0faTLKD9KNZa8GPaqDBwMN1+rqT1/4hDPup5rTF8Wk0jbA==')})
  }
//]]>
